  <script>
      (adsbygoogle = window.adsbygoogle || []).push({});

<script>
  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
      const micBtn = document.getElementById('micBtn');
      const searchInput = document.getElementById('searchInput');
      const searchForm = document.getElementById('searchForm');
  
      let mediaRecorder;
      let audioChunks = [];
      let isRecording = false;
  
      // Mic bosilganda
      micBtn.addEventListener('click', async () => {
          if (!isRecording) {
              // 1. YOZISHNI BOSHLASH
              startRecording();
          } else {
              // 2. YOZISHNI TO'XTATISH VA YUBORISH
              stopRecording();
          }
      });
  
      async function startRecording() {
          try {
              // Mikrofondan ruxsat so'rash
              const stream = await navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia({ audio: true });
              
              mediaRecorder = new MediaRecorder(stream);
              audioChunks = []; // Eski datani tozalash
  
              // Har safar ovoz bo'lagi kelganda yig'ib boramiz
              mediaRecorder.ondataavailable = event => {
                  audioChunks.push(event.data);
              };
  
              // Yozish to'xtaganda nima bo'lishi
              mediaRecorder.onstop = async () => {
                  // UI ni tozalash
                  micBtn.classList.remove('mic-listening');
                  micBtn.innerHTML = '<i class="ri-mic-line fs-5"></i>';
                  searchInput.placeholder = "Searching...";
  
                  // Audio fayl (Blob) yaratish
                  const audioBlob = new Blob(audioChunks, { type: 'audio/webm' });
                  
                  // Backendga yuborish
                  sendAudioToBackend(audioBlob);
              };
  
              // Yozishni boshlash
              mediaRecorder.start();
              isRecording = true;
              
              // UI o'zgarishi
              micBtn.classList.add('mic-listening');
              micBtn.innerHTML = '<i class="ri-stop-circle-line fs-4"></i>'; // Stop icon
              searchInput.placeholder = "speak up... (Press to stop)";
  
          } catch (err) {
              console.error("Mic Error:", err);
              // alert("Mikrofonni yoqib bo'lmadi.");
          }
      }
  
      function stopRecording() {
          if (mediaRecorder && mediaRecorder.state !== 'inactive') {
              mediaRecorder.stop(); // Bu 'onstop' eventini chaqiradi
              isRecording = false;
          }
      }
  
      async function sendAudioToBackend(audioBlob) {
          const formData = new FormData();
          // Fayl nomi 'voice_input'
          formData.append('voice_input', audioBlob, 'recording.webm');
  
          try {
              // Backend URL ga POST qilish
              const response = await fetch('/voice-search', {
                  method: 'POST',
                  body: formData
              });
  
              const data = await response.json();

              
              if (data.title) {
                  searchInput.value = data.title;
                  searchForm.submit();
              } else {
                  // alert("Ovozni tushunib bo'lmadi yoki xatolik: " + (data.error || 'Unknown'));
                  searchInput.placeholder = "Search artist, track or lyrics...";
              }
  
          } catch (error) {
              console.error("Server Error:", error);
              // alert("Serverga ulanishda xatolik bo'ldi");
              searchInput.placeholder = "Search artist, track or lyrics...";
          }
      }
  });
  </script>


<script>
  function changeSource(sourceName) {
      const urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
      const currentSource = urlParams.get('source') || 'shazam';
      
      if (currentSource !== sourceName) {
          window.location.href = window.location.pathname + "?source=" + sourceName;
      }
  }
</script>
